Darkness: using System.Linq; using System.Collections.Generic; using System;  namespace Oxide.Plugins {     [Info("DeployablesAutoRemover", "Rust Admin Community", "1.0.0")]     [Description("TBD")]     class DeployablesAutoRemover : RustPlugin     {         private const float REMOVE_INTERVAL = 30.0f;                  private enum DecayEntityPrefabs : uint         {             HighStoneWall = 1585379529u,             HighWoodenWall = 1745077396u,             HighIceWall = 921229511u,             LowIceWall = 797759041u,             LowGraveyardFence = 1766793357u,             StoneGate = 4211374971u,             WoodenGate = 95147612u,              // ..         }          private void OnServerInitialized()         {             foreach (var decayEntity in BaseNetworkable.serverEntities.OfType<DecayEntity>())             {                 TryHandle(decayEntity, (DecayEntity entity) =>                 {                     if (IsValidDecayEntity(entity))                     {                         RemoveDecayEntity(entity);                     }                 });             }         }          private static void TryHandle(DecayEntity entity, System.Action<DecayEntity> callback)         {             try { callback(entity); }             catch (NullReferenceException) { }         }          private static bool IsValidDecayEntity(DecayEntity entity)         {             return _DECAY_PREFABS.Contains((DecayEntityPrefabs)entity.prefabID)                 && entity.HasParent() == false;         }          private static readonly HashSet<DecayEntityPrefabs> _DECAY_PREFABS =             Enum.GetValues(typeof(DecayEntityPrefabs)).Cast<DecayEntityPrefabs>().ToHashSet();          private void OnEntitySpawned(DecayEntity decayEntity)         {             if (IsValidDecayEntity(decayEntity))             {                 ModifyDecayDelay(decayEntity);             }             else             {                 Puts($"OnEntitySpawned='{decayEntity.ShortPrefabName}', prefabID='{decayEntity.prefabID}u'");             }         }          private void RemoveDecayEntity(DecayEntity decayEntity)         {             decayEntity.KillMessage();         }          private void ModifyDecayDelay(DecayEntity decayEntity)         {             timer.Once(REMOVE_INTERVAL, () =>             {                 TryHandle(decayEntity, (DecayEntity entity) =>                 {                     if (entity.IsDestroyed == false)                     {                         RemoveDecayEntity(entity);                     }                 });             });         }     } }

I4IgO: // Reference: Facepunch.Ping  #if CARBON #else // Reference: 0Harmony #endif  using System; using Facepunch.Ping;  #if CARBON using HarmonyLib; #else using Harmony; #endif  namespace Oxide.Plugins {     [Info("Ping Estimator Fix", "rostov114", "0.1.0")]     class PingEstimatorFix : RustPlugin     { #if CARBON         private Harmony _harmony; #else         private HarmonyInstance _harmony; #endif          private static bool _hasCached;          #region Init         private void Init()         { #if CARBON             _harmony = new HarmonyLib.Harmony(Name + "PATCH");             _harmony.PatchAll(); #else             _harmony = HarmonyInstance.Create(Name + "PATCH");             Type[] patchType =             {                 AccessTools.Inner(typeof(PingEstimatorFix), "PingEstimater_RefreshCacheIfExpired"),             };             foreach (var t in patchType) { new PatchProcessor(_harmony, t, HarmonyMethod.Merge(t.GetHarmonyMethods())).Patch(); } #endif         }          private void Unload()         {             _harmony.UnpatchAll(Name + "PATCH"); //Unpatch harmony         }         #endregion          #region Harmony         [HarmonyPatch(typeof(PingEstimater), "RefreshCacheIfExpired")]         public static class PingEstimater_RefreshCacheIfExpired         {             [HarmonyPrefix]             public static bool Prefix()             {                 bool flag;                 if (_hasCached)                 {                     flag = false;                 }                 else                 {                     _hasCached = true;                     flag = true;                 }                  return flag;             }         }         #endregion     } }
